[2021/2/24-11:52-clip]	 export function attackRatedAbilityList(weight: number, animation: AnimationTrack, attackAbility: Ability, extraDuration: number = 0): AbilityOptionallyWithWeightOrTiming {
	const frame = 0.7

	return [
		weight,
		playAnimationAbility(animation, frame * 20),
		attackAbility,
		{
			debugName: `waitForCooldown`,
			abilityType: AbilityType.WAIT_FOR_COOLDOWN,
			durationInGameTicks: 0,
			validTargets: AbilityTargets.MYSELF,
			validTargetSelection: AbilityTargetSelectionStyle.ALL,
			timeAlready: frame
		},
		waitAbility(extraDuration)
	]
}

[2021/2/25-12:26-tab]	 calculate-rarity.ts - loot - Visual Studio Code
[2021/2/25-12:26-clip]	 export function getRarityByValue(rarityValue: number): ItemRarity {
	let itemRarity: ItemRarity
	if (rarityValue > ASTRONOMICAL_THRESHOLD) {
		itemRarity = ItemRarity.ASTRONOMICAL
	} else if (rarityValue > LEGENDARY_THRESHOLD) {
		itemRarity = ItemRarity.LEGENDARY
	} else if (rarityValue > EPIC_THRESHOLD) {
		itemRarity = ItemRarity.EPIC
	} else if (rarityValue > RARE_THRESHOLD) {
		itemRarity = ItemRarity.RARE
	} else if (rarityValue > UNCOMMON_THRESHOLD) {
		itemRarity = ItemRarity.UNCOMMON
	} else if (rarityValue > COMMON_THRESHOLD) {
		itemRarity = ItemRarity.COMMON
	} else {
		itemRarity = ItemRarity.COMMON
	}

	return itemRarity
}

[2021/2/25-16:29-clip]	 				if (projectile.nid === null) {
					// Skip any projectile we've deallocated in the pool
					return
				}
				// Don't check for collisions for enemy<->enemy projectiles
				if (projectile.targetType === ProjectileTargetType.PLAYER) {
					return
				}

				// Stop healers healing themselves
				if (projectile.owningEntityId === enemy.nid) {
					return
				}

				// Don't collide with dead entity colliders
				if (enemy.isDead() && !enemy.persistentCorpse) {
					return
				}

				debugDrawLine(enemy, projectile, 0xff0000)

				this.collisionsCheckedThisFrame++

				const hitCollider = this.ccdProjectileCollisionCheck(projectile, enemy.colliders)
				if (hitCollider) {
					let newCollision = false
					if (CCD) {
						if (!projectile.entitiesCollided.includes(enemy.nid) && !projectile.ignoreCollided.includes(enemy.nid)) {
							projectile.entitiesCollided.push(enemy.nid)
							newCollision = true
						}
					} else {
						const entity = find(projectile.entitiesHit, (entityHit) => {
							return entityHit.nid === enemy.nid
						})
						if (!entity) {
							projectile.entitiesHit.push({ nid: enemy.nid, projectileHitBy: [projectile.nid], piercedBy: [] })
							newCollision = true
						} else {
							entity.projectileHitBy.push(projectile.nid)
						}
					}

					if (newCollision) {
						this.projectileApplyOnHit(projectile, enemy)

						projectile.splashDamage = 0.1
						projectile.splashRadius = 1500

						if (!projectile.splashedAlready && projectile.splashDamage && projectile.splashRadius) {
							const projectileDamage = projectile.getDamageInstance()
							// only splash on first enemy hit
							const config = projectile.getChildProjectileConfig(false)
							config.colliderRadius = projectile.splashRadius

							const boomScale = config.colliderRadius * BOOM_SCALE_FACTOR

							const projectilePos = projectile.collider.pos
							const projectileDir = sub(projectilePos, projectile.collider.prevPosition).normalize()
							const projectileFront = projectilePos.clone().add(scale(projectileDir, projectile.collider.r))

							const hitPos = findIntersection(projectile.collider.prevPosition, projectileFront, hitCollider) || projectilePos

							createElementalAoeExplosionPfx(hitPos, projectile.getDamageInstance(), boomScale)

							enemy.takingHitCausedSplashDamageThisFrame = true

							this.addGroundHazardFn(projectile.owningEntity, projectile.targetType, hitPos, projectile.aimVector.clone(), config, projectileDamage.rawDamage * projectile.splashDamage, [...projectile.entitiesHit], [...projectile.entitiesCollided], true)
							projectile.splashedAlready = true
						}

						if (projectile.pierceCount > 0) {
							projectile.pierceCount--
						} else {
							projectile.toBeDeleted = true
						}
					}
				}
			})
